const LC = ["top", "right", "bottom", "left"],
    Qn = Math.min,
    it = Math.max,
    va = Math.round,
    ji = Math.floor,
    Xt = e => ({
        x: e,
        y: e
    }),
    DC = {
        left: "right",
        right: "left",
        bottom: "top",
        top: "bottom"
    },
    FC = {
        start: "end",
        end: "start"
    };
function au(e, t, n) {
    return it(e, Qn(t, n))
}
function fn(e, t) {
    return typeof e == "function" ? e(t) : e
}
function hn(e) {
    return e.split("-")[0]
}
function Io(e) {
    return e.split("-")[1]
}
function Nd(e) {
    return e === "x" ? "y" : "x"
}
function kd(e) {
    return e === "y" ? "height" : "width"
}
function Kn(e) {
    return ["top", "bottom"].includes(hn(e)) ? "y" : "x"
}
function Ed(e) {
    return Nd(Kn(e))
}
function zC(e, t, n) {
    n === void 0 && (n = !1);
    const r = Io(e),
        o = Ed(e),
        s = kd(o);
    let i = o === "x" ? r === (n ? "end" : "start") ? "right" : "left" : r === "start" ? "bottom" : "top";
    return t.reference[s] > t.floating[s] && (i = ya(i)), [i, ya(i)]
}
function $C(e) {
    const t = ya(e);
    return [lu(e), t, lu(t)]
}
function lu(e) {
    return e.replace(/start|end/g, t => FC[t])
}
function BC(e, t, n) {
    const r = ["left", "right"],
        o = ["right", "left"],
        s = ["top", "bottom"],
        i = ["bottom", "top"];
    switch (e) {
    case "top":
    case "bottom":
        return n ? t ? o : r : t ? r : o;
    case "left":
    case "right":
        return t ? s : i;
    default:
        return []
    }
}
function UC(e, t, n, r) {
    const o = Io(e);
    let s = BC(hn(e), n === "start", r);
    return o && (s = s.map(i => i + "-" + o), t && (s = s.concat(s.map(lu)))), s
}
function ya(e) {
    return e.replace(/left|right|bottom|top/g, t => DC[t])
}
function VC(e) {
    return {
        top: 0,
        right: 0,
        bottom: 0,
        left: 0,
        ...e
    }
}
function Vv(e) {
    return typeof e != "number" ? VC(e) : {
        top: e,
        right: e,
        bottom: e,
        left: e
    }
}
function xa(e) {
    const {x: t, y: n, width: r, height: o} = e;
    return {
        width: r,
        height: o,
        top: n,
        left: t,
        right: t + r,
        bottom: n + o,
        x: t,
        y: n
    }
}
function Eh(e, t, n) {
    let {reference: r, floating: o} = e;
    const s = Kn(t),
        i = Ed(t),
        l = kd(i),
        c = hn(t),
        u = s === "y",
        f = r.x + r.width / 2 - o.width / 2,
        p = r.y + r.height / 2 - o.height / 2,
        y = r[l] / 2 - o[l] / 2;
    let w;
    switch (c) {
    case "top":
        w = {
            x: f,
            y: r.y - o.height
        };
        break;
    case "bottom":
        w = {
            x: f,
            y: r.y + r.height
        };
        break;
    case "right":
        w = {
            x: r.x + r.width,
            y: p
        };
        break;
    case "left":
        w = {
            x: r.x - o.width,
            y: p
        };
        break;
    default:
        w = {
            x: r.x,
            y: r.y
        }
    }
    switch (Io(t)) {
    case "start":
        w[i] -= y * (n && u ? -1 : 1);
        break;
    case "end":
        w[i] += y * (n && u ? -1 : 1);
        break
    }
    return w
}
const HC = async (e, t, n) => {
    const {placement: r="bottom", strategy: o="absolute", middleware: s=[], platform: i} = n,
        l = s.filter(Boolean),
        c = await (i.isRTL == null ? void 0 : i.isRTL(t));
    let u = await i.getElementRects({
            reference: e,
            floating: t,
            strategy: o
        }),
        {x: f, y: p} = Eh(u, r, c),
        y = r,
        w = {},
        S = 0;
    for (let v = 0; v < l.length; v++) {
        const {name: g, fn: m} = l[v],
            {x: h, y: x, data: b, reset: C} = await m({
                x: f,
                y: p,
                initialPlacement: r,
                placement: y,
                strategy: o,
                middlewareData: w,
                rects: u,
                platform: i,
                elements: {
                    reference: e,
                    floating: t
                }
            });
        f = h ?? f,

function Xj(e, t) {
    const n = Math.abs(t.top - e.y),
        r = Math.abs(t.bottom - e.y),
        o = Math.abs(t.right - e.x),
        s = Math.abs(t.left - e.x);
    switch (Math.min(n, r, o, s)) {
    case s:
        return "left";
    case o:
        return "right";
    case n:
        return "top";
    case r:
        return "bottom";
    default:
        throw new Error("unreachable")
    }
}
function Zj(e, t, n=5) {
    const r = [];
    switch (t) {
    case "top":
        r.push({
            x: e.x - n,
            y: e.y + n
        }, {
            x: e.x + n,
            y: e.y + n
        });
        break;
    case "bottom":
        r.push({
            x: e.x - n,
            y: e.y - n
        }, {
            x: e.x + n,
            y: e.y - n
        });
        break;
    case "left":
        r.push({
            x: e.x + n,
            y: e.y - n
        }, {
            x: e.x + n,
            y: e.y + n
        });
        break;
    case "right":
        r.push({
            x: e.x - n,
            y: e.y - n
        }, {
            x: e.x - n,
            y: e.y + n
        });
        break
    }
    return r
}

function nN(e) {

        return e.slice();

        }

    }

    const n = [];

    })

function WE() {
    const [, e] = Ks(),
        {setUser: t} = Js(),
        {toast: n} = $a(),
        [r, o] = d.useState(""),
        [s, i] = d.useState(""),
        [l, c] = d.useState(""),
        [u, f] = d.useState(!1),
        p = async y => {
            if (y.preventDefault(), s !== l) {
                n({
                    variant: "destructive",
                    title: "Passwords don't match",
                    description: "Please make sure both passwords are the same"
                });
                return
            }
            if (s.length < 6) {
                n({
                    variant: "destructive",
                    title: "Password too short",
                    description: "Password must be at least 6 characters"
                });
                return
            }
            f(!0);
            try {
                const S = await (await xd("POST", "/api/auth/signup", {
                    username: r,
                    password: s
                })).json();
                t(S),
                n({
                    title: "Account created!",
                    description: "Let's get you set up"
                }),
                e("/onboarding")
            } catch (w) {
                n({
                    variant: "destructive",
                    title: "Signup failed",
                    description: w.message || "Username may already be taken"
                })
            } finally {
                f(!1)
            }
        };
    return a.jsx("div", {
        className: "min-h-screen flex items-center justify-center bg-gradient-to-b from-background to-muted/20 p-4",
        children: a.jsxs("div", {
            className: "w-full max-w-md space-y-6",
            children: [a.jsxs("div", {
                className: "flex items-center gap-4",
                children: [a.jsx(jo, {
                    href: "/welcome",
                    children: a.jsx(ce, {
                        variant: "ghost",
                        size: "icon",
                        "data-testid": "button-back",
                        children: a.jsx(Cv, {
                            className: "w-5 h-5"
                        })
                    })
                }), a.jsxs("div", {
                    className: "flex items-center gap-2 text-primary",
                    children: [a.jsx(Eo, {
                        className: "w-8 h-8"
                    }), a.jsx("h1", {
                        className: "text-2xl font-bold",
                        children: "GlyPal"
                    })]
                })]
            }), a.jsxs(re, {
                children: [a.jsxs(el, {
                    children: [a.jsx(tl, {
                        children: "Create Your Account"
                    }), a.jsx(nl, {
                        children: "Join GlyPal to start your wellness journey"
                    })]
                }), a.jsx(ei, {
                    children: a.jsxs("form", {
                        onSubmit: p,
                        className: "space-y-4",
                        children: [a.jsxs("div", {
                            className: "space-y-2",
                            children: [a.jsx(te, {
                                htmlFor: "username",
                                children: "Username"
                            }), a.jsx(ke, {
                                id: "username",
                                type: "text",
                                value: r,
                                onChange: y => o(y.target.value),
                                required: !0,
                                "data-testid": "input-username"
                            })]
                        }), a.jsxs("div", {
                            className: "space-y-2",
                            children: [a.jsx(te, {
                                htmlFor: "password",
                                children: "Password"
                            }), a.jsx(ke, {
                                id: "password",
                                type: "password",
                                value: s,
                                onChange: y => i(y.target.value),
                                required: !0,
                                minLength: 6,
                                "data-testid": "input-password"
                            })]
                        }), a.jsxs("div", {
                            className: "space-y-2",
                            children: [a.jsx(te, {
                                htmlFor: "confirm-password",
                                children: "Confirm Password"
                            }), a.jsx(ke, {
                                id: "confirm-password",
                                type: "password",
                                value: l,
                                onChange: y => c(y.target.value),
                                required: !0,
                                minLength: 6,
                                "data-testid": "input-confirm-password"
                            })]
                        }), a.jsx(ce, {
                            type: "submit",
                            className: "w-full",
                            disabled: u,
                            "data-testid": "button-submit",
                            children: u ? "Creating account..." : "Create Account"
                        }), a.jsxs("p", {
                            className: "text-center text-sm text-muted-foreground",
                            children: ["Already have an account?", " ", a.jsx(jo, {
                                href: "/login",
                                className: "text-primary hover:underline",
                                "data-testid": "link-login",
                                children: "Sign in"
                            })]
                        })]
                    })
                })]
            })]
        })
    })
}
const QE = ["Dairy", "Eggs", "Fish", "Shellfish", "Tree Nuts", "Peanuts", "Wheat", "Soy", "Sesame"],
    KE = ["Lactose", "Gluten", "Fructose", "Histamine", "FODMAPs"],
    GE = ["American", "Italian", "Mexican", "Asian", "Mediterranean", "Indian", "Japanese", "Thai", "French", "Middle Eastern"];
function qE() {
    const [, e] = Ks(),
        {user: t, setUser: n} = Js(),
        {toast: r} = $a(),
        [o, s] = d.useState(1),
        [i, l] = d.useState(!1),
        [c, u] = d.useState({
            locale: "en-US",
            birth_year: new Date().getFullYear() - 40,
            units: "imperial",
            sex_at_birth: "Prefer not to say",
            height_ft: 5,
            height_in: 8,
            height_cm: 173,
            weight_lb: 160,
            weight_kg: 72.5,
            activity_level: "sedentary",
            goal: "maintain",
            goal_intensity_pct: 15,
            dietary_pattern: "No preference",
            allergies: [],
            intolerances: [],
            cross_contam_may_contain: !1,
            cross_contam_shared_equipment: !1,
            cross_contam_shared_facility: !1,
            cuisines: [],
            time_per_meal: "30 min",
            cooking_skill: "Beginner",
            budget_tier: "Moderate",
            carb_exchange_g: 15,
            bg_low: 70,
            bg_high: 180,
            bg_urgent: 250
        }),
        f = (g, m) => {
            u(h => ({
                ...h,
                [g]: m
            }))
        },
        p = (g, m) => {
            u(h => {
                const x = h[g],
                    b = x.includes(m) ? x.filter(C => C !== m) : [...x, m];
                return {
                    ...h,
                    [g]: b
                }
            })
        },
        y = g => {
            g !== c.units && u(m => {
                if (g === "metric") {
                    const h = m.height_ft * 12 + m.height_in,
                        x = Math.round(h * 2.54),
                        b = Math.round(m.weight_lb * .453592 * 10) / 10;
                    return {
                        ...m,
                        units: g,
                        height_cm: x,
                        weight_kg: b
                    }
                } else {
                    const h = Math.round(m.height_cm / 2.54),
                        x = Math.floor(h / 12),
                        b = h % 12,
                        C = Math.round(m.weight_kg / .453592);
                    return {
                        ...m,
                        units: g,
                        height_ft: x,
                        height_in: b,
                        weight_lb: C
                    }
                }
            })
        },
        w = () => {
            if (o === 1 && c.birth_year < 1900) {
                r({
                    variant: "destructive",
                    title: "Missing information",
                    description: "Please enter a valid birth year"
                });
                return
            }
            s(g => g + 1)
        },
        S = () => {
            s(g => g - 1)
        },
        v = async () => {
            if (t) {
                l(!0);
                try {
                    await xd("POST", "/api/me/onboarding", {
                        userId: t.id,
                        locale: c.locale,
                        birth_year: c.birth_year,
                        units: c.units,
                        sex_at_birth: c.sex_at_birth,
                        height: {
                            ft: c.units === "imperial" ? c.height_ft : void 0,
                            in: c.units === "imperial" ? c.height_in : void 0,
                            cm: c.units === "metric" ? c.height_cm : void 0
                        },
                        weight_lb: c.units === "imperial" ? c.weight_lb : void 0,
                        weight_kg: c.units === "metric" ? c.weight_kg : void 0,
                        activity_level: c.activity_level,
                        goal: c.goal,
                        goal_intensity_pct: c.goal === "maintain" ? void 0 : c.goal_intensity_pct / 100,
                        dietary_pattern: c.dietary_pattern,
                        allergies: c.allergies,
                        intolerances: c.intolerances,
                        cross_contam: {
                            may_contain: c.cross_contam_may_contain,
                            shared_equipment: c.cross_contam_shared_equipment,
                            shared_facility: c.cross_contam_shared_facility
                        },
                        cuisines: c.cuisines,
                        time_per_meal: c.time_per_meal,
                        cooking_skill: c.cooking_skill,
                        budget_tier: c.budget_tier,
                        carb_exchange_g: c.carb_exchange_g,
                        bg_thresholds: {
                            low: c.bg_low,
                            high: c.bg_high,
                            urgent: c.bg_urgent
                        }
                    });
                    const g = {
                        ...t,
                        onboardingCompleted: !0
                    };
                    n(g),
                    r({
                        title: "Welcome to GlyPal!",
                        description: "Your profile is all set up"
                    }),
                    e("/")
                } catch (g) {
                    r({
                        variant: "destructive",
                        title: "Failed to save profile",
                        description: g.message || "An error occurred"
                    })
                } finally {
                    l(!1)
                }
            }
        };
    return a.jsx("div", {
        className: "min-h-screen flex items-center justify-center bg-gradient-to-b from-background to-muted/20 p-4",
        children: a.jsxs("div", {
            className: "w-full max-w-2xl space-y-6",
            children: [a.jsxs("div", {
                className: "flex items-center gap-2 text-primary justify-center",
                children: [a.jsx(Eo, {
                    className: "w-8 h-8"
                }), a.jsx("h1", {
                    className: "text-2xl font-bold",
                    children: "GlyPal"
                })]
            }), a.jsxs(re, {
                children: [a.jsx(el, {
                    children: a.jsxs("div", {
                        className: "flex items-center justify-between",
                        children: [a.jsxs("div", {
                            children: [a.jsxs(tl, {
                                children: [o === 1 && "Basic Information", o === 2 && "Health Profile", o === 3 && "Activity & Goals", o === 4 && "Dietary Restrictions", o === 5 && "Food Preferences", o === 6 && "Cooking & Budget", o === 7 && "Blood Glucose Settings"]
                            }), a.jsxs(nl, {
                                children: ["Step ", o, " of 7"]
                            })]
